<p>There are many companies out there, some are only offering support until your website is done, while some companies offer do-it-yourself services. With DatastiQ, we will carefully study your personal / business needs and walk with you, hand-in-hand, until we reach your destination and even with your next journey.</p></div>

<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>From the moment you successfully signed up, your hosting and domain name will be up and running immediately.</p>
<p>For the Web Design service, it would usually take weeks to months. There is no definite time because, in order for us to successfully build your website, we would also need You! The most important person who needs to be engaged in this project is yourself. This is because you know the business, you know what you need and what to put on your website.</p>
<p>Our Business Analysts and Web Developers will strongly rely on you on contents, themes, and images from your business. You need to invest in photography and capture every product, brand and even moments to fully personalize your website.</p></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_10  et_pb_toggle_close">
<h5 class="et_pb_toggle_title">What is Cloud Hosting?</h5>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>Cloud hosting is where your website is hosted on a cluster of servers instead of having your site hosted on one server. In case of an issue, your site can be migrated to another server. In simple terms, it makes a copy of your site on different servers, including to the ones near to your visitors, therefore allowing faster loading time as they don’t need to access it from the main server.</p></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_11  et_pb_toggle_close">
<h5 class="et_pb_toggle_title">What is LightSpeed Web Server?</h5>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>LiteSpeed web server is a high-performance Apache drop-in replacement. LSWS is the 4th most popular web server on the internet and the #1 commercial web server. Performance up to 9x faster than Apache with a small memory footprint and increased scalability. Full benefits on the official <a href="https://www.litespeedtech.com/products/litespeed-web-server">LSWS website.</a></p></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_12  et_pb_toggle_close">
<h5 class="et_pb_toggle_title">Where is your Data Center located?</h5>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>Our datacenter is located in Lansing, Michigan, United States of America. You can also determine this by running Who.Is using our IP Address. <a href="https://who.is/whois-ip/ip-address/67.227.186.45">Click here to run the test.</a></p></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_13  et_pb_toggle_close">
<h5 class="et_pb_toggle_title">Conventional Hosting vs Cloud Hosting?</h5>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>Conventional or traditional hosting may promise 99.99% uptimes, however, it is challenging to live up to that. One major reason for this is the shared nature of the services. If one website experiences unprecedented high traffic, it could cause downtime issues with all the websites on that server.</p>
<p>Cloud hosting, on the other hand, has impeccable uptimes since the users are on a dedicated server. Even though there is an aspect of shared resources, problems on one server only mean websites are moved to another functioning server.</p></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_14  et_pb_toggle_close">
<h5 class="et_pb_toggle_title">What is SSD?</h5>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>It stands for Solid State Drives. Our private cloud has been built using Solid State Drives protected by Raid 10. Solid state drives don’t have any moving parts and they use flash memory to store data, which provides much better performance and reliability over conventional Hard Disk Drives (HDD). RAID 10, also known as RAID 1+0, combines disk mirroring and disk striping to protect data.</p></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_15  et_pb_toggle_close">
<h5 class="et_pb_toggle_title">Do you offer free SSL certificate?</h5>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>All domains and sub-domains hosted on our Web Hosting accounts come with free and automatic SSL (https) powered by <a href="https://letsencrypt.org/">Let’s Encrypt</a>. Let’s Encrypt is a free, automated, and open certificate authority (CA), run for the public’s benefit. It is a service provided by the Internet Security Research Group (ISRG).</p></div>
</div><div class="et_pb_toggle et_pb_module et_pb_accordion_item et_pb_accordion_item_16  et_pb_toggle_close">
<h5 class="et_pb_toggle_title">Does your hosting plans have limits?</h5>
<div class="et_pb_toggle_content clearfix"><p>We believe transparency is key to a successful relationship working together. Below is our standard account limits:</p>
<ul>
<li>CPU: Intel(R) Xeon(R)</li>
<li>CPUs: 100% Of 1 Full CPU Core</li>
<li>Disk Space: Based on the plan selected</li>
<li>Bandwidth: Unlimited Bandwidth</li>
<li>Virtual Memory: 2048MB (2GB)</li>
<li>Physical Memory: 1024MB (1GB)</li>
<li>Concurrent Connections: 25</li>
<li>Number of Processes: 100</li>
<li>I/O Limit: 2048KB/s</li>
<li>I/O operations per second: 1024</li>
<li>Inodes: 100,000 to 250,000*</li>
</ul>
<p><span style="font-size: 14px;">*Please note: You can request to increase your Inodes, however, accounts over 100,000 Inodes or 20GB disk aren’t included in daily backups.</span></p></div>
</div>
</div>
